Allow the oil to heat, then add the onion and peppers to the skillet. Saute until softened and beginning to brown, 6-7 minutes. Add the black beans, green chiles, garlic, salt, black pepper, cumin, coriander, and oregano to the skillet. Cook until fragrant, 1-2 minutes longer.","Transfer the bean mixture to a mixing bowl. Gently mash the beans with a large fork, leaving some whole.","Place a few tortillas on a dinner plate and warm in a microwave until pliable, 20-30 seconds. Repeat until all tortillas are soft and pliable.","Spoon about 1/4 cup of the bean mixture into the center of a tortilla. Gently roll the tortilla and place it seam side down in the sauce in the casserole dish. Repeat with the remaining tortillas.","Pour remaining enchilada sauce evenly over the rolled tortillas, spreading the sauce to make sure all tortillas are covered. (Pro tip: Include a sprinkling of vegan cheese over the top if you'd like.)","Cover the dish with a sheet of aluminum foil.","Bake the enchiladas on the middle rack of the oven for 20 minutes.","Remove foil and continue baking until edges are bubbling, 7-10 minutes.","Check to see that enchiladas are done.
